      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jacqueline's Reads by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/20694309-jade-leigh">Jade Leigh</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=6-stars-top-favorites">6-stars-top-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer725697484" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10168305992614024859"><b>FREE! - > <a href='http://www.smashwords.com/books/view/283554' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a></b><br/><br/><a href='http://imgur.com/lUtATKK' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380849040i/3134165._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>If you haven’t read any of Tijan books, then I’m here to tell you, <u>stop what you are doing and pick one up</u>. Yep, just do it, go put the word “Tijan” in your search box on Amazon and then do your one click thing, b/c you will get your money’s worth and then some.</b><br/><br/>Oh I should warn you, this review will be filled with major fan girl moments. Do I have a crush on Tijan? Maybe. I would like to take this moment to thank all the people that have pushed me to read this book. I even had </span>
  <span id="freeText10168305992614024859" style="display:none"><b>FREE! - &gt; <a href="http://www.smashwords.com/books/view/283554" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/lUtATKK" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380849040i/3134165._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>If you haven’t read any of Tijan books, then I’m here to tell you, <u>stop what you are doing and pick one up</u>. Yep, just do it, go put the word “Tijan” in your search box on Amazon and then do your one click thing, b/c you will get your money’s worth and then some.</b><br><br>Oh I should warn you, this review will be filled with major fan girl moments. Do I have a crush on Tijan? Maybe. I would like to take this moment to thank all the people that have pushed me to read this book. I even had an author bestie tell me. Yeah, I have an author bestie, she doesn’t know that b/c I’m like stalker, but anyhow, she told me to read Fallen Crest High several times and so I finally did.<br><br><b>I FUCKING LOVED FALLEN CREST HIGH!</b><br><br>Oh I loved Mason<br><br>I loved every-single page.<br><br>If I could make love to a book, I would. TMI? I will reframe and will go on with the review now.<br><br><b>DISCLAIMER - &gt; THIS IS NOT A LOVE TRIANGLE BOOK. This is about two brothers and a girl. It’s filled with 100% adorable, laugh-out-loud cuteness.</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/ocGmSzI" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380849040i/3134166._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Cheaters are weak. They’re selfish and they’re cowards. No, I’m not a cheater and I never intend to be.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Samantha’s (Sam) mother just told Sam that her parents are getting a divorce. Sam and her mother will be shacking it up with the man her mother cheated with. Sucks right? So Sam has to move in with her mother’s lover and guess what?! He has two sons. Shocker. The two sons are Mason and Logan. All three kids don’t want anything to do with each other. Mason and Logan go to Fallen Crest Public and Sam goes to Fallen Crest Academy, they are rival schools.<br><br>Okay, so that is just the TIP of what the book is about. Look, I don’t want to go all into it, but let me break it down for you by my personal opinion of the characters and then my overall feelings.<br><br><b>Sam</b><br><br>Sam is an incredible, strong, awesome and a little bitchy Heroine. I love her. I usually don’t like bitchy Heroines, but damn it, I secretly want to be her. There’s a lot of shit she has to do deal with. She’s got her dysfunctional family, friend problems and people treating her bad at school. You want to give the girl a hug, but really she doesn’t need it b/c she’s like fucking tough.<br><br><b>Logan</b><br><br>Oh lord, he’s funny, strong, and a major asshole. Logan is the type of guy you just want to watch a movie with because he will talk the entire time talking and make you laugh the entire time. If you think funny is sexy, then that’s Logan.<br><br><b>Mason</b><br><br>Where do I begin with him. SIGH. My author bestie told me I would love him b/c he’s a major brute, alpha male (yadda yadda) you know what I mean and damn, she’s right. I LOVE Mason. He is a book boyfriend and yes I even have dreams about him. Just half the shit he does in the book, you are thinking to yourself, Mason, can you do that to me?! He’s arrogant, broody and kind of mysterious, but in the end he’s passionate and loyal. Um… yes please.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/XvLLSar" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380849040i/3134167.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He was sculpted as a statue. The added comfort he had with his body, which he didn’t give a damn if he were naked or wore clothes, took my breath away.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This was my first Tijan read and it will not be the last. I finished this book at 2AM and I started book 2 right away. I’m that much of a psycho. You guys get it. When I love something, I love it to the fullest and I will admit to you now, I loved this book and I love the author.<br><br><b>READ THIS BOOK and then message me so we can talk about it.</b><br><br>For more reviews, visit - &gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com">http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com</a><br></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" href="/user/show/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b">It&#39;s just me Shelly B</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer4972254610726813069">I didn't get the fascination with this book.<br/>The plot is confusing. The writing is horrible. I couldn't tell what was going on half the time in the book because alot of it was going on at once and it didn't make sense. The main characters were weird and seriously, describing someone having a 'hyena laugh' does not make that guy gorgeous. <br/>I didn't understand Mason and Logan. Honestly, I thought they were creeps ad bullies. They tortured people and bullied good guys like Adam and the author went ar</span>
  <span id="freeText4972254610726813069" style="display:none">I didn't get the fascination with this book.<br />The plot is confusing. The writing is horrible. I couldn't tell what was going on half the time in the book because alot of it was going on at once and it didn't make sense. The main characters were weird and seriously, describing someone having a 'hyena laugh' does not make that guy gorgeous. <br />I didn't understand Mason and Logan. Honestly, I thought they were creeps ad bullies. They tortured people and bullied good guys like Adam and the author went around and tagged Adam as a bad guy? WHAT THE FUCK. This story was CONFUSING. I still didn't understand the half of it. <br />And the drama, OH MY GOD! It was ridiculous. Basically the heroine Sam, is dating her step brother Mason. But people think she's dating her other step brother and Mason's real brother, Logan who apparently likes her too. I don't know what the fuck's with that because Logan never seemed to like her but treated her as a sister in the whole story. Then, we find out Sam's mom and Mason and Logan's dad are going to get married. Sam's biological dad and Mason and Logan's mom are getting married. Sam's father who raised her is marrying one of Sam's classmate, mark's mom. I mean, seriously! TOO MUCH FUCKING DRAMA WHICH DIDN'T MAKE SENSE. I didn't get the point of hooking up Logan with Sam's school's QUEEN BITCH, Miranda so that Logan could be happy and forget about Sam? WHAT THE FUCK IS HAPPENING IN THIS BOOK. I didn't understand the story. Or the characters. <br />And every 10 pages and Sam goes of running for 4 hours at a stretch. <br />And the love between Mason and Sam? WHEN THE FUCK DID THAT HAPPEN?!?!?!? They were barely together in the book. Then they ended up having sex once. Then twice. Then no contact for a week. then again sex. And then they said I love you's to each other. <br />URGHHHH!! NEVER BEEN SO FUCKING PISSED AT A BOOK BEFORE!<br />I HATED THIS BOOK. HATED IT. NEVER EVEN BOTHER READING THIS. I ONLY GAVE IT 2 STARS BECAUSE IT HAD A CLIFFHANGER ENDING AND IT GOT ME A BIT CURIOUS. </span>

  <u>Second re-read: 24.05.2018</u>
</b><br>Somehow, I still like this book. <b>Samantha ‘Sam’ Jacquelyn Strattan</b> (17) is almost, <i>almost</i> like me. I, too, struggle to feel, what she does to numb the pain; running, I do with reading books. We both have the <i>‘I just don't care’</i> feeling/mood(?), so that's probably why I'd get along with her. <b>Mason ‘Mase’ James Kade</b> (18?) is still fucking hot. I love how he's in control, not scared, always having the upper hand, always being the powerful one, and he is a somewhat dominant alpha male; just my type. I'd read this book all over again just to be with him <i>again</i>. <b>Overall, I'm not really all that surprised that I still like it</b>. It's a interesting book, with hot sex scenes and all that. Still something is of course missing from making this book a fantastic story. But the rating went a little bit down this time around. The rating seems to go up and down for me...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I didn’t care. As I drove away, I sat back. I really didn’t care, about any of it. And I knew in the back of my mind, far far in the back of my mind, that this wasn’t the healthiest feeling. But then again, I didn’t care.</i>
  </b>

Mason’s narrowed. And I sneered at him before I went inside to pay. When I came back out, Lydia and Jessica were still in the bathroom; Mason passed me to pay inside. He wore a black leather jacket over a black shirt and jeans. His black hair was cut short and his eyes held mine in some form of trance as he passed by me. His jacket rubbed against me, he passed so close, and we both turned to watch the other.<br>My heart faltered for a moment.<br>The same hatred I felt for him was in his eyes.<br>Fuck him.</i></b></blockquote>
<br><blockquote>―――――――――――――――――――――――――――――――――――――</blockquote>
<br><blockquote><b><i>I ducked my head and pulled the top on. When it fit like a glove, just above my jeans, I leaned forward to inspect my face in the mirror. I wasn’t anything great, long black hair, thin with a runner’s build, and eyes that were bleak.<br>“Samantha, honey, I worry about you. No one stands a chance.”<br>I grinned at him. “What about Nate?”<br>He tapped his beer with mine. “When he's around, it's the foursome fearsome. You can add any 'some to that name. Thank goodness, huh?” Then he groaned.“I really need to get laid tonight.”</i></b></blockquote>

<br><blockquote><b><i>“People are snakes, you just have to figure out their different colors, but they're all the same. Everybody wants something.” </i></b></blockquote>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I hadn’t seen the Kade brothers up close, not in a long time, but I’d heard plenty about them. Logan was a junior, like me. Mason was a year older. Both were good looking and Mason was rumored to be six foot one with a muscular build. He played defensive lineman for a reason on his football team. Logan had the leaner build, but he was an inch shorter.<br>I snorted to myself. I couldn’t believe I even knew these details. As I cursed my friends inside for their gossiping ways, I glanced back at the Escalade and froze once more. Two green eyes stared back at me.<br>Mason had been filling up his vehicle and watching me the whole time.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Other characters</u>:</b><br><i>I've put these in a spoilers tag simply because it's a long as list.</i><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>↦ <b>Logan Kade</b> (17?), Mason's brother. And they go to Fallen Crest Public High school and both brothers played for the school football team. He, according to Sam, has quite a hyena laugh. Though it bugged me the second time re-reading this book, I never wrote about it in the review, this time however... it really annoyed me. I kept think of The Lion King when the hyenas laugh.... not a pretty sight when Logan is supposed to be this hot, sexy guy. Didn't work with the image. <br>↦ <b>Nate Monson</b> (18?), Mason's best friend and Logan's friend.<br>↦ <b>James Kade</b>, the Kade brothers father. Not a good father.<br>↦ <b>Analise ‘Lise’</b>, Sam's mother. Bad, bad mother.<br>↦ <b>David Strattan</b>, Sam's father (though not biological father) and coach for the football team at a private school; Fallen Crest Academy. He should've fought more for Sam. Proven to her that, though he isn't her biological father, he <i>is</i> her father as he raised her.<br>↦ <b>Garrett Brickshire</b>, Sam's biological father, the hotshot lawyer from Boston. Seems like a cool dude, though perhaps a selfish one?<br>↦ <b>Helen</b>, the Kade brothers mother. Not sure how I feel about this woman. She is kinda a bitch, like Sam's mother. A different kind of bitch?<br>↦ <b>Jeffrey ‘Jeff’ Sallaway</b>, Sam's ex. They dated for three years. <b>Jessica ‘Jess’ Larsen</b> and <b>Lydia Thompson</b>, Sam's <s>friends</s> from school. Jess has been fooling around with Jeff behind Sam's back for over two years, Lydia hid it. <b>Jill Flatten</b>, an enemy of Sam, now dating Jeff after Sam broke up with him. Lydia tries to be a better friend to Sam eventually, Jessica still hates her.<br>↦ <b>Adam Quinn</b>, Academy team’s quarterback. Has a crush on Sam. Uses Becky to get to her. <b>Ashley DeCortts</b>, his ex-girlfriend.<br>↦ <b>Rebecca ‘Becky’ Sallaway</b>, Jeff’s cousin only through marriage. Sam's somewhat friend. She has a major crush on Adam, but think herself not worthy of him. <br>↦ <b>Malinda Decraw</b>, She was the single mother of Mark Decraw; one of Becky’s termed Academy Elite. He was co-captain. She seems interested in David; they start dating.<br>↦ <b>Miranda Stewart</b>, Fallen Academy’s elite queen bee. <b>Cassandra Sullivan</b>, <b>Emily Connsway</b>, <b>Peter Glasburg</b>, <b>Amelia White</b>, <b>Mark Decraw</b>; members of the group. Adam is in it too. - Miranda's with Peter. Cass wants Adam. Amelia and Mark seems to be dating.<br>↦ <b>Marissa</b>, a good friend of Mason. He protective of her because he's the reason she had to switch schools a couple years ago.<br>↦ <b>Tate</b>, Logan's ex of two years. She tried to come between Mason and his brother; she used Logan to get to Mason. That’s why he hate the bitch, but Logan still loves her. Which is why he has a soft spot for her. <b>Tanya</b>, Tate' cousin.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i> “I don’t care. I can’t handle this. My game is talk. You tried to take that away.” He shot an arm towards Mason. “He fights. I talk. That’s the magic of our twosome fearsome. Sam’s one of us, man. She’s got the guts to do the dirty deeds if we don’t. She watches out for us too. Ya’ll are stupid if you didn’t see this coming.” He thrust his arms out wide. “The three of us are a magical team. No way are you screwing this up.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Young Adult) Contemorary Romance.<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book One.<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[HFN. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Mason Kade.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Sure.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Probably. <br><b>New Rating</b> - 3.5 stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>Re-read: 17.08.15</u>
</b><br>I'm shocked. I like this way better the second time around, in fact, I think I loved it! I L O V E Mason!<br><b>New rating: 4 stars.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>First read: 20.05.14</u>
</b><br>This series wasn't really so bad. I'm surprised that I enjoyed it as much as I did. I do love a bad boy alpha... and Mason is all that.<br><b>Rate: 3/4 stars.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4621057302347958882">This book was awesome! Boy, was it filled with so much drama and I was riveted to it all. I’m so glad I did not go to high school with these people. They would just rather eat you up and spit you out.<br/><br/>I started this book with some false assumptions that had me doubting the real reasons behind a few actions. That made me hesitant about some of these characters until I realized I was wrong. I loved Mason, Sam, Logan and Nate. Their loyalty to each other is what I truly love to read about.<br/><br/>Mason is t</span>
  <span id="freeText4621057302347958882" style="display:none">This book was awesome! Boy, was it filled with so much drama and I was riveted to it all. I’m so glad I did not go to high school with these people. They would just rather eat you up and spit you out.<br /><br />I started this book with some false assumptions that had me doubting the real reasons behind a few actions. That made me hesitant about some of these characters until I realized I was wrong. I loved Mason, Sam, Logan and Nate. Their loyalty to each other is what I truly love to read about.<br /><br />Mason is the silent broody type of Hero that I adore. Sam was the I don’t give a f*** heroine I rarely find in books. Logan was the life of the party. I wondered if he was on speed throughout most of this book, but I loved him for it. Nate wasn’t in the book too much but he made an impact regardless. <br /><br />The rest of the characters were bitches and I gleefully enjoyed them getting stomped on. I probably shouldn’t admit that... Yep, I’m hooked.<br /><br /></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=childhood-loves">childhood-loves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=listened-to-audio-version">listened-to-audio-version</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16384209-candace?shelf=rich-guys">rich-guys</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer664751821" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3708157692954649828">I think I've found a new guilty pleasure! Holy hell, I couldn't break away from this story! It was packed with catty girls, high school drama, shallow social-climbers and pubescent douchebags...And don't get me started on the adults! Yet, despite finding nearly all of them to be pretty appalling, I was completely addicted! What a ride!<br/><br/>I won't recap this one because so many others have done such a wonderful job already. I'll just say that this book was definitely worth it. I had my doubts, since </span>
  <span id="freeText3708157692954649828" style="display:none">I think I've found a new guilty pleasure! Holy hell, I couldn't break away from this story! It was packed with catty girls, high school drama, shallow social-climbers and pubescent douchebags...And don't get me started on the adults! Yet, despite finding nearly all of them to be pretty appalling, I was completely addicted! What a ride!<br /><br />I won't recap this one because so many others have done such a wonderful job already. I'll just say that this book was definitely worth it. I had my doubts, since high school melodrama gets old so quick, but I only wish I'd read this book earlier. Sam, Logan and Mason are great characters and I loved them almost immediately. The various parental figures definitely kept this story interesting, with their selfish actions and destructive behaviors.<br /><br />Don't make the same mistake as me, by putting this one off. It is fabulous!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9745440694282295764"><b> 4 Awesomely screwed up stars!</b><br/><br/>The first thing that comes to my mind when I think about this book is that these characters are completely messed up. And considering the amount of books I read and the amout of crazy characters with whom I cross, that’s saying A LOT. Nonetheless, I just couldn’t put it down.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429452ra/860352.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Samantha has a screw up life.   <span id="freeText9745440694282295764" style="display:none"><b> 4 Awesomely screwed up stars!</b><br><br>The first thing that comes to my mind when I think about this book is that these characters are completely messed up. And considering the amount of books I read and the amout of crazy characters with whom I cross, that’s saying A LOT. Nonetheless, I just couldn’t put it down.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429452ra/860352.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Samantha has a screw up life. She has a shitty cheater boyfriend and cheaters girl-friends. And to top that her mom suddenly resolves to divorce her father and go live with another man. But nooooo, not just any man: James Kade, the dearest father of Mason and Logan Kade, the most popular and famous brothers in town. <br>Hot, sexy and rich bad boys either you want to be them or want to be <i>with</i> them.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429452i/860353._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Somehow they end up putting Sam under their wings and along the way, Mason and Sam start to grow feelings very far from “brotherly”. Which is not good considering that they soon going to be step-brothers. <br>But then again, their families are completely f***ed up, so it’s not that weird, considering all that happens inside it. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380429452i/860354.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can’t tell you more because this book is crazy. Crazy, I tell you. There’s always something completely screwed up happening. Almost everyone is a bitch or an asshole and the hole “high-school-secret-popularity-hierarchy” is in full force. <br>And the adults in this book are even more messed up than the teenagers. Talk about crazy folks! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380429452ra/860355.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So yeah, basically this book is awesome. Sam is awesome and really don’t care about anything that is thrown at her, Mason is hot in a discreet way and Logan is pretty sexy and cool too. <br>It’s a really addictive book and you just HAVE to read it. ;)</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/509202848?book_show_action=true">Jan 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer509202848" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1883260723729865831"><b>Holy High School Drama!</b><br/><br/>When Samantha’s parent’s divorce, she finds herself moving in with mom’s new finance and his two sons, Mason and Logan Kade. Samantha attends the local private school and the Kade brothers are gods at the local public school. They are worshipped for their performance on the football field as well as being every girl in towns dream guys.<br/><br/>Samantha faces a lot of drama amongst her friends and boyfriend Jeff as well as coming to terms with a lot of bombs mom repeatedly drops on</span>
  <span id="freeText1883260723729865831" style="display:none"><b>Holy High School Drama!</b><br /><br />When Samantha’s parent’s divorce, she finds herself moving in with mom’s new finance and his two sons, Mason and Logan Kade. Samantha attends the local private school and the Kade brothers are gods at the local public school. They are worshipped for their performance on the football field as well as being every girl in towns dream guys.<br /><br />Samantha faces a lot of drama amongst her friends and boyfriend Jeff as well as coming to terms with a lot of bombs mom repeatedly drops on her throughout the story. To the shock of all her peers and family the Kade boys take her under their wing and makes her one of them. Samantha finds true friendship and love within the “Kade fold” and stands up for herself time and time again. <br /><br />The parents in this book are seriously messed up and make terrible decisions. With the love and support of the Logan and Mason, Samantha makes it through all the craziness.<br /><br />Mason Kade’s is hot, broody and all out town god and is head over heels for Samantha. They have hot chemistry and I’m excited to see where their relationship goes in the next book!!<br /><br /><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('3EvZ88G05wHc2NFi9tgxalHfL/F/XzNnL0CBbOnG1t20x+yXlKSdRr3k2AB1YDevUJQFscnnYeh8FuqKLj+QAw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }
